## <span id="11">1.1 前言</span>

### <span id="111">1.1.1 什么是虚拟化？</span>

在计算机技术中，虚拟化（技术）或虚拟技术（英语：Virtualization）是一种资源管理技术，是将计算机的各种实体资源（CPU、内存、磁盘空间、网络适配器等），予以抽象、转换后呈现出来并可供分区、组合为一个或多个电脑配置环境。

<p align="center">
  &nbsp;<img data-original="https://clsn.io/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/1190037-20180127150319319-1411302318.png" src="/wp-content/themes/clsn-003/img/blank.gif" alt="KVM 虚拟化技术" alt="" />
</p>

<p align="center">
  图 - 虚拟化示意图
</p>

由此，打破实体结构间的不可切割的障碍，使用户可以比原本的配置更好的方式来应用这些电脑硬件资源。这些资源的新虚拟部分是不受现有资源的架设方式，地域或物理配置所限制。

一般所指的虚拟化资源包括计算能力和数据存储。

由于目前信息技术领域的很多企业都曾在宣传中将该企业的某种技术称为虚拟化技术，这些技术涵盖的范围可以从<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Java</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;">虚拟机技术</span>到<span style="text-decoration: underline;">系统管理软件</span>，这就使得准确的界定虚拟技术变得困难。因此各种相关学术论文在谈到虚拟技术时常常提到的便是如前面所提到的那个不严格的定义。

### <span id="112">1.1.2 为什么要用虚拟化</span>

　　?同一台物理机运行多个不同版本应用软件

　　?硬件依赖性较低和便于数据迁移

<p align="center">
  <img data-original="https://clsn.io/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/1190037-20180127150333537-2034113371.png" src="/wp-content/themes/clsn-003/img/blank.gif" alt="KVM 虚拟化技术" alt="" />
</p>

<p align="center">
  图 - 虚拟化前后对比
</p>

&nbsp;&nbsp; 详情参考<1.1.3 虚拟化技术的优势>。

### <span id="113">1.1.3 虚拟化技术的优势</span>

<span style="color: #99cc00;"><strong>　　1.</strong><strong>降低运营成本</strong></span>

　　服务器虚拟化降低了IT基础设施的运营成本，令系统管理员摆脱了繁重的物理服务器、OS、中间件及兼容性的管理工作，减少人工干预频率，使管理更加强大、便捷。

<span style="color: #99cc00;"><strong>　　2.</strong><strong>提高应用兼容性</strong></span>

　　服务器虚拟化提供的封装性和隔离性使大量应用独立运行于各种环境中，管理人员不需频繁根据底层环境调整应用，只需构建一个应用版本并将其发布到虚拟化后的不同类型平台上即可。

<span style="color: #99cc00;"><strong>　　3.</strong><strong>加速应用部署</strong></span>

　　采用服务器虚拟化技术只需输入激活配置参数、拷贝虚拟机、启动虚拟机、激活虚拟机即可完成部署，大大缩短了部署时间，免除人工干预，降低了部署成本。

<span style="color: #99cc00;"><strong>　　4.</strong><strong>提高服务可用性</strong></span>

　　用户可以方便地备份虚拟机，在进行虚拟机动态迁移后，可以方便的恢复备份，或者在其他物理机上运行备份，大大提高了服务的可用性。

<span style="color: #99cc00;"><strong>　　5.</strong><strong>提升资源利用率</strong></span>

　　通过服务器虚拟化的整合，提高了CPU、内存、存储、网络等设备的利用率，同时保证原有服务的可用性，使其安全性及性能不受影响。

<span style="color: #99cc00;"><strong>　　6.</strong><strong>动态调度资源</strong></span>

　　在服务器虚拟化技术中，数据中心从传统的单一服务器变成了统一的资源池，用户可以即时地调整虚拟机资源，同时数据中心管理程序和数据中心管理员可以灵活根据虚拟机内部资源使用情况灵活分配调整给虚拟机的资源。

<span style="color: #99cc00;"><strong>　　7.</strong><strong>降低能源消耗</strong></span>

　　通过减少运行的物理服务器数量，减少CPU以外各单元的耗电量，达到节能减排的目的。

### <span id="114_KVM">1.1.4 KVM简介</span>

<p align="center">
  <img data-original="https://clsn.io/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/1190037-20180127150445600-1123409281.png" src="/wp-content/themes/clsn-003/img/blank.gif" alt="KVM 虚拟化技术" alt="" />
</p>

　　KVM，基于内核的虚拟机（英语：_Kernel-based Virtual Machine_，缩写为 KVM），是一种用于Linux内核中的虚拟化基础设施，可以将Linux内核转化为一个hypervisor。KVM在2007年2月被导入Linux 2.6.20核心中，以可加载核心模块的方式被移植到FreeBSD及illumos上。

　　KVM在具备Intel VT或AMD-V功能的x86平台上运行。它也被移植到S/390，PowerPC与IA-64平台上。在Linux内核3.9版中，加入ARM架构的支持。

　　KVM目前由Red Hat等厂商开发，对CentOS/Fedora/RHEL等Red Hat系发行版支持极佳。

### <span id="115_KVM">1.1.5 关于KVM</span>

>   1. KVM是开源软件，全称是kernel-based virtual machine（基于内核的虚拟机）。
>   2. 是x86架构且硬件支持虚拟化技术（如 intel VT 或 AMD-V）的Linux全虚拟化解决方案。
>   3. 它包含一个为处理器提供底层虚拟化 可加载的核心模块kvm.ko（kvm-intel.ko或kvm-AMD.ko）。
>   4. KVM还需要一个经过修改的QEMU软件（qemu-kvm），作为虚拟机上层控制和界面。
>   5. KVM能在不改变linux或windows镜像的情况下同时运行多个虚拟机，（它的意思是多个虚拟机使用同一镜像）并为每一个虚拟机配置个性化硬件环境（网卡、磁盘、图形适配器&hellip;&hellip;）同时KVM还能够使用ksm技术帮助宿主服务器节约内存。
>   6. 在主流的Linux内核，如2.6.20以上的内核均已包含了KVM核心。

### <span id="116_Virtual_Machine_Manager">1.1.6 关于Virtual Machine Manager</span>

　　在电脑运算中，红帽公司的Virtual Machine Manager是一个虚拟机管理员，可以让用户管理多个虚拟机。

　　基于内核的虚拟机libvirt与<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Virtual Machine Manager</span>。&nbsp;

<span style="background-color: #00ff00;"><strong>Virtual Machine Manager</strong></span>**可以让用户**：

　　? 创建、编辑、引导或停止虚拟机。

　　? 查看并控制每个虚拟机的控制台。

　　? 查看每部虚拟机的性能以及使用率。

　　? 查看每部正在运行中的虚拟机以及主控端的即时性能及使用率信息。

　　? 不论是在本机或远程，皆可使用KVM、Xen、QEMU。

<p align="center">
  <img data-original="https://clsn.io/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/1190037-20180127150534084-1372550304.png" src="/wp-content/themes/clsn-003/img/blank.gif" alt="KVM 虚拟化技术" alt="" />
</p>

<p align="center">
  图 -&nbsp; libvirt服务
</p>

### <span id="117">1.1.7 其他虚拟化软件</span>

**? Xen**

　　Xen是一个开放源代码虚拟机监视器，由XenProject开发。它打算在单个计算机上运行多达128个有完全功能的操作系统。

　　在旧（无虚拟硬件）的处理器上执行Xen，<span style="text-decoration: underline;">操作系统必须进行显式地修改（</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;">&ldquo;</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;">移植</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;">&rdquo;</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;">）以在</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;">Xen</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;">上运行（但是提供对用户应用的兼容性）</span>。这使得Xen无需特殊硬件支持，就能达到高性能的虚拟化。

**? QEMU**

　　QEMU是一套由Fabrice Bellard所编写的模拟处理器的自由软件。它与Bochs，PearPC近似，但其具有某些后两者所不具备的特性，如高速度及跨平台的特性。经由KVM（早期为kqemu加速器，现在kqemu已被KVM取代）这个开源的加速器，QEMU能模拟至接近真实电脑的速度。QEMU有两种主要运作模式：

**　　<span style="text-decoration: underline;">User mode</span>****模拟模式**，亦即是用户模式。

　　QEMU能引导那些为不同中央处理器编译的Linux程序。而Wine及Dosemu是其主要目标。

**　　<span style="text-decoration: underline;">System mode</span>****模拟模式**，亦即是系统模式。

　　QEMU能模拟整个电脑系统，包括中央处理器及其他周边设备。它使得为系统源代码进行测试及除错工作变得容易。其亦能用来在一部主机上模拟数部不同虚拟电脑。

## <span id="12_KVM">1.2 KVM部署与使用</span>

系统环境说明

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> cat /etc/redhat-release </span>
CentOS Linux release 7.4.1708<span style="color: #000000;"> (Core) 
[root@kvm </span>~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> uname -r</span>
3.10.0-693<span style="color: #000000;">.el7.x86_64
[root@kvm </span>~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> sestatus </span>
<span style="color: #000000;">SELinux status:                 disabled
[root@kvm </span>~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> systemctl status firewalld.service </span>
● firewalld.service - firewalld -<span style="color: #000000;"> dynamic firewall daemon
   Loaded: loaded (</span>/usr/lib/systemd/system/<span style="color: #000000;">firewalld.service; disabled; vendor preset: enabled)
   Active: inactive (dead)
     Docs: man:firewalld(</span>1<span style="color: #000000;">)
[root@kvm </span>~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> hostname -I</span>
172.16.1.240 10.0.0.240
<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> kvm主机内存不能低于4GB</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

### <span id="121_KVM">1.2.1 安装KVM虚拟化软件</span>

安装依赖包(可以使用本地yum源)

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>yum install libvirt* virt-* qemu-kvm* -y</pre>
  </div>
</div>

安装软件说明内容：

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>libvirt    <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 虚拟机管理</span>
virt       <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 虚拟机安装克隆</span>
qemu-kvm   <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 管理虚拟机磁盘</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

启动服务

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> systemctl start libvirtd.service</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> systemctl status libvirtd.servic</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

安装VNC软件：

　　下载vnc软件方法，tightvnc官网：[http://www.tightvnc.com][1]

　　<span style="text-decoration: underline;">VNC软件，用于VNC（Virtual Network Computing）</span>，为一种使用RFB协议的显示屏画面分享及远程操作软件。此软件借由网络，可发送键盘与鼠标的动作及即时的显示屏画面。

　　VNC与操作系统无关，因此可跨平台使用，例如可用Windows连接到某Linux的电脑，反之亦同。甚至在没有安装客户端程序的电脑中，只要有支持JAVA的浏览器，也可使用。

　　安装VNC时，使用默认安装即可，无需安装server端。

<p align="center">
  &nbsp;<img data-original="https://clsn.io/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/1190037-20180127150727850-800432127.png" src="/wp-content/themes/clsn-003/img/blank.gif" alt="KVM 虚拟化技术" alt="" />
</p>

<p align="center">
  图 - vnc软件
</p>

### <span id="122_KVM">1.2.2 配置第一台KVM虚拟机</span>

使用命令

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virt-install --virt-type kvm --os-type=linux --os-variant rhel7 --name centos7 --memory 1024 --vcpus 1 --disk /data/clsn.raw,format=raw,size=10 --cdrom /data/CentOS-7-x86_64-DVD-1511.iso --network network=default --graphics vnc,listen=0.0.0.0,port=5900 --noautoconsole</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

**　<span style="color: #ff0000;">　注意：</span>**需要先将镜像文件拷贝到 /data/CentOS-7-x86_64-DVD-1511.iso 。

<p style="text-align: left;">

</p>

    <td style="width: 43.34%; border: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-themetint: 153; border-top: none; mso-border-top-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-top-themetint: 153; mso-border-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; background: #EAF1DD; mso-background-themecolor: accent3; mso-background-themetint: 51; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" width="43%">
      <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph; mso-yfti-cnfc: 68;">
        <strong><span lang="EN-US">--noreboot<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></strong>
      </p>
    </td>
    
    <td style="width: 56.66%; border-top: none; border-left: none; border-bottom: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-bottom-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-bottom-themetint: 153; border-right: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-right-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-right-themetint: 153; mso-border-top-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-top-themetint: 153; mso-border-left-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-left-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-left-themetint: 153; mso-border-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-themetint: 153; background: #EAF1DD; mso-background-themecolor: accent3; mso-background-themetint: 51; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" width="56%">
      <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph; mso-yfti-cnfc: 64;">
        <span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New';">安装完成后不启动客户机。</span>
      </p>
    </td>
  </tr>
  
  <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 21; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes;">
    <td style="width: 100.0%; border: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-themetint: 153; border-top: none; mso-border-top-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-top-themetint: 153; mso-border-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; background: #92D050; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" colspan="2" width="100%">
      <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph; mso-yfti-cnfc: 4;">
        <span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">以上信息通过</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> <span lang="EN-US">" virt-install --help " </span></span><span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">获得。</span>
      </p>

&nbsp;　　在启动的同时使用vnc连接

      </p>

    <td style="width: 70.22%; border-top: none; border-left: none; border-bottom: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-bottom-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-bottom-themetint: 153; border-right: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-right-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-right-themetint: 153; mso-border-top-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-top-themetint: 153; mso-border-left-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-left-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-left-themetint: 153; mso-border-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-themetint: 153; background: #EAF1DD; mso-background-themecolor: accent3; mso-background-themetint: 51; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" valign="top" width="70%">
      <p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-yfti-cnfc: 64;">
        <span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New';">取消虚拟机开机启动</span>
      </p>
    </td>
  </tr>
  
  <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 17; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes;">
    <td style="width: 100.0%; border: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-themetint: 153; border-top: none; mso-border-top-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-top-themetint: 153; mso-border-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" colspan="2" valign="top" width="100%">
      <p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-yfti-cnfc: 4;">
        <strong><span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New';">以上参数通过</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New';">&ldquo;</span><span lang="EN-US">virsh<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>--help</span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New';">&rdquo;</span> </strong><strong><span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New';">获得。</span></strong>
      </p>
    </td>
  </tr>
</table>

<span style="background-color: #00ffff;">操作过程：</span>

KVM虚拟机配置文件位置

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> ll /etc/libvirt/qemu/centos7.xml</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

修改KVM虚拟机配置的方法

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh edit centos7</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

&nbsp;&nbsp; 使用该命令修改可以对文件进行语法校验。

<span style="background-color: #00ff00;"><strong>备份与恢复</strong></span>

**备份虚拟机配置(关机时备份):**

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh dumpxml centos7  > centos7.xml</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

**删除虚拟机配置**

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 查看</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh list --all </span>
<span style="color: #000000;"> Id    名称                         状态
</span>----------------------------------------------------
 -<span style="color: #000000;">     centos7                        关闭
 </span><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 删除</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh undefine centos7 </span>
<span style="color: #000000;">域 centos7 已经被取消定义
[root@kvm </span>~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh list --all </span>
<span style="color: #000000;"> Id    名称                         状态
</span>----------------------------------------------------</pre>
  </div>
</div>

**导入虚拟机**

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 导入</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh define centos7-off.xml </span>
定义域 centos7（从 centos7-<span style="color: #000000;">off.xml）
</span><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 查看</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh list --all </span>
<span style="color: #000000;"> Id    名称                         状态
</span>----------------------------------------------------
 -     centos7                        关闭</pre>
  </div>
</div>

**修改虚拟机名称**

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 重命名</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh domrename centos7 clsn7</span>
<span style="color: #000000;">Domain successfully renamed
</span><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 查看</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh list</span>
<span style="color: #000000;"> Id    名称                         状态
</span>----------------------------------------------------
 9     clsn7                          关闭</pre>
  </div>
</div>

**虚拟机挂起与恢复**

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 挂起虚拟机</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh suspend clsn7</span>
<span style="color: #000000;">域 clsn7 被挂起
</span><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 查看状态</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh list --all</span>
<span style="color: #000000;"> Id    名称                         状态
</span>----------------------------------------------------
 9     clsn7                          暂停</pre>
  </div>
</div>

恢复虚拟机

<div class="cnblogs_code">
  <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh resume clsn7 </span>
域 clsn7 被重新恢复</pre>
</div>

<span style="background-color: #00ff00;"><strong>查询虚拟机vnc</strong><strong>端口</strong></span>

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh vncdisplay clsn7 </span>
<span style="color: #000000;">:0  
</span><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> :0 即 为 5900 端口，以此类推 :1为5901 。</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

**开机自启动设置**

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 设置 libvirtd 服务开机自启动。</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> systemctl is-enabled libvirtd.service </span>
enabled</pre>
  </div>
</div>

&nbsp;&nbsp; 设置宿主机开机虚拟机在其他

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh autostart clsn7 </span>
<span style="color: #000000;">域 clsn7标记为自动开始
</span><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 实质为创建软连接</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> ll /etc/libvirt/qemu/autostart/clsn7.xml </span>
lrwxrwxrwx 1 root root 27 1月  22 12:17 /etc/libvirt/qemu/autostart/clsn7.xml -> /etc/libvirt/qemu/clsn7.xml</pre>
  </div>
</div>

取消开机自启动

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh autostart --disable clsn7 </span>
域 clsn7取消标记为自动开始</pre>
  </div>
</div>

## <span id="13_kvmconsole">1.3 kvm虚拟机console登录</span>

### <span id="131_CentOS_7X_console">1.3.1 CentOS 7.X 版本console登录</span>

配置console登录

在clsn7虚拟机内操作(该操作<span style="color: #ff0000;"><strong>仅限</strong></span><span style="color: #ff0000;"><strong>centos7</strong></span>)：

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> grubby --update-kernel=ALL --args="console=ttyS0,115200n8"</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> reboot</span><span style="color: #008000;">
#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 115200n8：能显示虚拟机的启动过程</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

重启完成后，使用virsh console 连接虚拟机。

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh console clsn7 </span>
<span style="color: #000000;">连接到域 clsn7
换码符为 </span>^<span style="color: #000000;">]
CentOS Linux </span>7<span style="color: #000000;"> (Core)
Kernel </span>3.10.0-327<span style="color: #000000;">.el7.x86_64 on an x86_64

clsn7 login: root
Password: 
Last login: Mon Jan </span>22 12:24:48 <span style="color: #0000ff;">from</span> 192.168.122.1<span style="color: #000000;">
[root@clsn7 </span>~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> w</span>
 12:26:11 up 0 min,  1 user,  load average: 0.09, 0.03, 0.01<span style="color: #000000;">
USER     TTY      FROM             LOGIN@   IDLE   JCPU   PCPU WHAT
root     ttyS0                     </span>12:26    3.00s  0.02s  0.01s w</pre>
  </div>
</div>

### <span id="132_CentOS_6X_console">1.3.2 CentOS 6.X 版本console登录</span>

使用virsh console连接CentOS 6虚拟主机方法：

　　安装一台centos6的kvm虚拟机

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>virt-install --virt-type kvm --os-type=linux --os-<span style="color: #000000;">variant rhel6 \
</span>--name clsn6 --memory 1124 --vcpus 1<span style="color: #000000;"> \
</span>--disk /data/clsn6/clsn-6.raw,format=raw,size=10<span style="color: #000000;"> \
</span>--cdrom /data/CentOS-6.9-x86_64-bin-<span style="color: #000000;">DVD1.iso \
</span>--network network=default --graphics vnc,listen=0.0.0.0,port=5901<span style="color: #000000;"> \
</span>--noautoconsole</pre>
  </div>
</div>

　　新安装一台虚拟机后，是无法通过virsh console 命令连入虚拟机中的，这时我们需要开启虚拟机的console功能。

<span style="color: #ff0000;">　　<span style="background-color: #ffff00;">以下操作都在虚拟机中进行</span></span>

1、添加ttyS0的许可，允许root登陆

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@clsn6 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> echo "ttyS0" >> /etc/securetty </span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

2、编辑/etc/grub.conf中加入console=ttyS0

&nbsp;&nbsp; 在该文件的第16行。kernel选项后添加

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@clsn6 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> sed -i '/\tkernel/s#.*#& console=ttyS0#g' /etc/grub.conf</span>
[root@clsn6 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> sync  # 同步配置到 /boot/grub/grub.conf</span>
[root@clsn6 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> cat -n  /etc/grub.conf </span>
     1    <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> grub.conf generated by anaconda</span>
     2    <span style="color: #008000;">#
</span>     3    <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> Note that you do not have to rerun grub after making changes to this file</span>
     4    <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> NOTICE:  You have a /boot partition.  This means that</span>
     5    <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;">          all kernel and initrd paths are relative to /boot/, eg.</span>
     6    <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;">          root (hd0,0)</span>
     7    <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;">          kernel /vmlinuz-version ro root=/dev/vda3</span>
     8    <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;">          initrd /initrd-[generic-]version.img</span>
     9    <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;">boot=/dev/vda</span>
    10    default=<span style="color: #000000;">0
    </span>11    timeout=5
    12    splashimage=(hd0,0)/grub/<span style="color: #000000;">splash.xpm.gz
    </span>13<span style="color: #000000;">    hiddenmenu
    </span>14    title CentOS 6 (2.6.32-696<span style="color: #000000;">.el6.x86_64)
    </span>15<span style="color: #000000;">        root (hd0,0)
    </span>16        kernel /vmlinuz-2.6.32-696.el6.x86_64 ro root=UUID=48532582-c271-4c0a-b55f-395fe16cd8aa rd_NO_LUKS rd_NO_LVM LANG=en_US.UTF-8 rd_NO_MD SYSFONT=latarcyrheb-sun16 crashkernel=auto  KEYBOARDTYPE=pc KEYTABLE=us rd_NO_DM rhgb quiet<span style="color: #ff0000;"> console=ttyS0
    17        initrd /initramfs-2.6.32-696.el6.x86_64.img</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

3、编辑/etc/inittab

　　在最后一行加入内容 S0:12345:respawn:/sbin/agetty ttyS0 115200

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@clsn6 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> echo 'S0:12345:respawn:/sbin/agetty ttyS0 115200' >>/etc/inittab</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

4、以上操作都完成后，重启虚拟机

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@clsn6 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> reboot</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

　　<span style="background-color: #ffff00; color: #ff0000;">以下操作在kvm宿主机上执行</span>

1、检查虚拟机的状态

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh list --all</span>
<span style="color: #000000;"> Id    名称                         状态
</span>----------------------------------------------------
 11<span style="color: #000000;">    clsn7                          running
 </span>21    clsn6                          running</pre>
  </div>
</div>

2、进行连接测试

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh console clsn6 </span>
<span style="color: #000000;">连接到域 clsn6
换码符为 </span>^]  <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 注：退出virsh console连接的方法，使用组合键Ctrl+]即可</span>
<span style="color: #000000;">
CentOS release </span>6.9<span style="color: #000000;"> (Final)
Kernel </span>2.6.32-696<span style="color: #000000;">.el6.x86_64 on an x86_64

clsn6 login: root
Password: 
Last login: Mon Jan </span>22 05:44:25<span style="color: #000000;"> on ttyS0
[root@clsn6 </span>~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> who</span>
root     ttyS0        2018-01-22 05:50
<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 登陆成功，查看登陆接口为之前设置的ttyS0</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

## <span id="14_KVM">1.4 KVM虚拟机磁盘、快照与克隆</span>

### <span id="141">1.4.1 磁盘管理</span>

　　KVM qcow2、raw、vmdk等镜像格式说明：[http://blog.csdn.net/zhengmx100/article/details/53887162][3]

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 创建一块qcow2的虚拟硬盘(<span style="color: #ff0000;">仅测试使用，无实际意义</span>)</span>
[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> qemu-img create -f qcow2 clsn.qcow2 2G</span>
[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> ls -l</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

查看当前虚拟机硬盘信息

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> qemu-img info /data/clsn.raw </span>
image: /data/<span style="color: #000000;">clsn.raw
file format: raw
virtual size: 10G (</span>10737418240<span style="color: #000000;"> bytes)
disk size: </span>1.1G</pre>
  </div>
</div>

**<span style="background-color: #ffff00;">raw</span>**<span style="background-color: #ffff00;"><strong>转qcow2</strong><strong>格式：</strong></span>

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 参数说明</span>
[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> qemu-img  --help |grep convert </span>
qemu-img convert [-f fmt] [-O output_fmt] filename  output_filename</pre>
  </div>
</div>

转换原有磁盘格式

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> qemu-img convert -f raw -O qcow2 clsn.raw clsn.qcow2</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

修改clsn7 虚拟机配置文件

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh edit clsn7 </span>
<span style="color: #000000;">修改前：
    </span>&lt;disk type=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">file</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> device=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">disk</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>>
      &lt;driver name=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">qemu</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> type=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">raw</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
      &lt;source file=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">/data/clsn.raw</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
      &lt;target dev=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">vda</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> bus=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">virtio</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
      &lt;address type=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">pci</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> domain=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x0000</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> bus=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x00</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> slot=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x06</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> function=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x0</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
    &lt;/disk><span style="color: #000000;">
修改后：
    </span>&lt;disk type=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">file</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> device=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">disk</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>>
      &lt;driver name=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">qemu</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> type=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">qcow2</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
      &lt;source file=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">/data/clsn.qcow2</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
      &lt;target dev=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">vda</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> bus=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">virtio</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
      &lt;address type=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">pci</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> domain=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x0000</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> bus=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x00</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> slot=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x06</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> function=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x0</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
    &lt;/disk></pre>
  </div>
</div>

删除原磁盘文件

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> \rm clsn.raw</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

启动虚拟机

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh start clsn7 </span>
<span style="color: #000000;">
[root@kvm data]</span><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh list --all </span>
<span style="color: #000000;"> Id    名称                         状态
</span>----------------------------------------------------
 22    clsn7                          running</pre>
  </div>
</div>

### <span id="142_KVM">1.4.2 KVM虚拟机添加硬盘</span>

进入硬盘存放目录

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> cd /data</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

创建一块新的硬盘

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> qemu-img create -f qcow2 clsn7-add01.qcow2 5G </span>
Formatting <span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">clsn7-add01.qcow2</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>, fmt=qcow2 size=5368709120 encryption=off cluster_size=65536 lazy_refcounts=off </pre>
  </div>
</div>

查看创建的硬盘信息

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> qemu-img info clsn7-add01.qcow2 </span>
image: clsn7-<span style="color: #000000;">add01.qcow2
file format: qcow2
virtual size: </span>5.0G (5368709120<span style="color: #000000;"> bytes)
disk size: 196K
cluster_size: </span>65536<span style="color: #000000;">
Format specific information:
    compat: </span>1.1<span style="color: #000000;">
    lazy refcounts: false</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

为虚拟机添加硬盘

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh attach-disk clsn7 /data/clsn7-add01.qcow2 vdb --live --cache=none --subdriver=qcow2</span><span style="color: #008000;">
#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 成功附加磁盘</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

参数说明：

  <o:RelyOnVML/>

 </o:OfficeDocumentSettings>

    <td style="width: 64.8%; border-top: none; border-left: none; border-bottom: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-bottom-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-bottom-themetint: 153; border-right: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-right-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-right-themetint: 153; mso-border-top-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-top-themetint: 153; mso-border-left-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-left-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-left-themetint: 153; mso-border-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-themetint: 153; background: #EAF1DD; mso-background-themecolor: accent3; mso-background-themetint: 51; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" width="64%">
      <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph; mso-yfti-cnfc: 64;">
        <span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New';">驱动类型</span>
      </p>
    </td>
  </tr>
</table>

<span style="background-color: #ffff00;"><strong>调整已添加硬盘的大小</strong></span>

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh --help |grep disk </span>
    attach-disk                    <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;">附加磁盘设备</span>
    detach-disk                    <span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;">分离磁盘设备</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

将已挂载的磁盘卸载下来

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh detach-disk clsn7  vdb </span>
成功分离磁盘</pre>
  </div>
</div>

调整磁盘大小

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 使用参数</span>
[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> qemu-img --help |grep resize</span>
  resize [-q] filename [+ | -]size</pre>
  </div>
</div>

&nbsp;&nbsp; 增加1G容量

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> qemu-img resize clsn7-add01.qcow2 +1G</span>
<span style="color: #000000;">Image resized.
[root@kvm data]</span><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> qemu-img info clsn7-add01.qcow2 </span>
image: clsn7-<span style="color: #000000;">add01.qcow2
file format: qcow2
virtual size: </span>6.0G (6442450944<span style="color: #000000;"> bytes)
disk size: 260K
cluster_size: </span>65536<span style="color: #000000;">
Format specific information:
    compat: </span>1.1<span style="color: #000000;">
    lazy refcounts: false</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

重新讲磁盘添加到虚拟机

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh attach-disk clsn7 /data/clsn7-add01.qcow2 vdb --live --cache=none --subdriver=qcow2</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

**　<span style="background-color: #ffff00; color: #ff0000;">　<span style="text-decoration: underline;">以下在虚拟机中操作</span></span>**

格式化磁盘

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@clsn7 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> mkfs.xfs /dev/vdb </span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

挂载磁盘

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@clsn7 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> df -h |grep /dev/vdb</span>
/dev/vdb        6.0G   33M  6.0G   1% /opt    </pre>
  </div>
</div>

使用 **<span style="text-decoration: underline;">xfs_growfs </span>**刷新磁盘的信息

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@clsn7 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> xfs_growfs --help </span>
xfs_growfs: invalid option -- <span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">-</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #000000;">
Usage: xfs_growfs [options] mountpoint</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

### <span id="143">1.4.3 快照管理</span>

**　<span style="color: #ff0000;">　注意:</span>**raw格式的磁盘无法创建快照

创建快照

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh snapshot-create clsn7 </span>
已生成域快照 1516607756</pre>
  </div>
</div>

查看主机快照列表

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh snapshot-list  clsn7</span>
<span style="color: #000000;"> 名称               生成时间              状态
</span>------------------------------------------------------------
 1516607756           2018-01-22 15:55:56 +0800<span style="color: #000000;"> running
</span><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 注：该名称为unix时间戳(格林威治时间)</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

查看快照信息

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh snapshot-info  clsn7 --snapshotname 1516607756</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

登陆虚拟机，进行删除操作

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@clsn7 /]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> ls -1|egrep -v 'proc|sys|run' |rm -rf</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

还原快照

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh snapshot-revert clsn7 --snapshotname 1516607756</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

删除快照

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh snapshot-delete  clsn7 --snapshotname 1516607756</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

快照配置文件位置

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> cd  /var/lib/libvirt/qemu/snapshot/</span>
[root@kvm snapshot]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> tree</span>
<span style="color: #000000;">.
└── clsn7
    └── </span>1516607756.xml</pre>
  </div>
</div>

### <span id="144_kvm">1.4.4 kvm虚拟机克隆</span>

　　复制一个虚拟机，需修改如 MAC 地址，名称等所有主机端唯一的配置。

　　虚拟机的内容并没有改变：virt-clone 不修改任何客户机系统内部的配置，它只复制磁盘和主机端的修改。所以像修改密码，修改静态 IP 地址等操作都在本工具复制范围内。如何修改此类型的配置，请参考 virt-sysprep。

　　克隆常用命令：

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virt-clone --auto-clone -o clsn7 </span>
<span style="color: #000000;">WARNING  设置图形设备端口为自动端口，以避免相互冲突。
正在分配 &lsquo;clsn</span>-clone.ra 4% [-                 ] 1.5 MB/s | 464 MB  01:50:18 ETA</pre>
  </div>
</div>

参数说明:

<table class="MsoTable15Grid4Accent3" style="width: 100.0%; border-collapse: collapse; border: none; mso-border-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-themetint: 153; mso-yfti-tbllook: 1184; mso-padding-alt: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" border="1" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
  <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: -1; mso-yfti-firstrow: yes; mso-yfti-lastfirstrow: yes;">
    <td style="width: 50.0%; border: solid #9BBB59 1.0pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; border-right: none; mso-border-top-alt: solid #9BBB59 .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-left-alt: solid #9BBB59 .5pt; mso-border-left-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid #9BBB59 .5pt; mso-border-bottom-themecolor: accent3; background: #9BBB59; mso-background-themecolor: accent3; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" width="50%">
      <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center; mso-yfti-cnfc: 5;" align="center">
        <strong><span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; color: white; mso-themecolor: background1;">参数</span></strong>
      </p>
    </td>
    
    <td style="width: 50.0%; border: solid #9BBB59 1.0pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; border-left: none; mso-border-top-alt: solid #9BBB59 .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid #9BBB59 .5pt; mso-border-bottom-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-right-alt: solid #9BBB59 .5pt; mso-border-right-themecolor: accent3; background: #9BBB59; mso-background-themecolor: accent3; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" width="50%">
      <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center; mso-yfti-cnfc: 1;" align="center">
        <strong><span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; color: white; mso-themecolor: background1;">参数说明</span></strong>
      </p>
    </td>
  </tr>
  
  <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 0;">
    <td style="width: 50.0%; border: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-themetint: 153; border-top: none; mso-border-top-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-top-themetint: 153; mso-border-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; background: #EAF1DD; mso-background-themecolor: accent3; mso-background-themetint: 51; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" width="50%">
      <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph; mso-yfti-cnfc: 68;">
        <strong><span lang="EN-US">--auto-clone<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></strong>
      </p>
    </td>
    
    <td style="width: 50.0%; border-top: none; border-left: none; border-bottom: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-bottom-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-bottom-themetint: 153; border-right: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-right-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-right-themetint: 153; mso-border-top-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-top-themetint: 153; mso-border-left-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-left-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-left-themetint: 153; mso-border-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-themetint: 153; background: #EAF1DD; mso-background-themecolor: accent3; mso-background-themetint: 51; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" width="50%">
      <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph; mso-yfti-cnfc: 64;">
        <span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New';">从原始客户机配置中自动生成克隆名称和存储路径。</span>
      </p>
    </td>
  </tr>
  
  <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 1; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes;">
    <td style="width: 50.0%; border: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-themetint: 153; border-top: none; mso-border-top-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-top-themetint: 153; mso-border-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" width="50%">

        <strong><span lang="EN-US">-o ORIGINAL_GUEST, </span></strong>
      </p>
      
      <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph; mso-yfti-cnfc: 4;">
        <strong><span lang="EN-US">--original ORIGINAL_GUEST</span></strong>
      </p>
    </td>
    
    <td style="width: 50.0%; border-top: none; border-left: none; border-bottom: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-bottom-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-bottom-themetint: 153; border-right: solid #C2D69B 1.0pt; mso-border-right-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-right-themetint: 153; mso-border-top-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-top-themetint: 153; mso-border-left-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-left-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-left-themetint: 153; mso-border-alt: solid #C2D69B .5pt; mso-border-themecolor: accent3; mso-border-themetint: 153; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;" width="50%">
      <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
        <span style="font-family: '微软雅黑',sans-serif; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New';">原始客户机名称；必须为关闭或者暂停状态。</span>
      </p>
    </td>
  </tr>
</table>

## <span id="15_kvm">1.5 kvm虚拟机网络管理</span>

### <span id="151">1.5.1 桥接网络配置</span>

1、设置桥接网络

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh iface-bridge eth0 br0</span>
<span style="color: #000000;">使用附加设备 br0 生成桥接 eth0 失败
已启动桥接接口 br0</span></pre>
  </div>
  
  <p>
    &nbsp;　　<span style="background-color: #ffff00;"><strong>查看网卡配置文件</strong></span>
  </p>
</div>

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 查看 eth0 配置文件</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> cat /etc/sysconfig/network-scripts/ifcfg-eth0</span>
DEVICE=<span style="color: #000000;">eth0
ONBOOT</span>=<span style="color: #000000;">yes
BRIDGE</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">br0</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span>
<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 查看 br0 配置文件</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> cat /etc/sysconfig/network-scripts/ifcfg-br0 </span>
DEVICE=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">br0</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
ONBOOT</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">yes</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
TYPE</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">Bridge</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
BOOTPROTO</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">none</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
IPADDR</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">10.0.0.240</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
NETMASK</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">255.255.255.0</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
GATEWAY</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">10.0.0.254</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
IPV6INIT</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">yes</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
IPV6_AUTOCONF</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">yes</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
DHCPV6C</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">no</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
STP</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">on</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
DELAY</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;"></span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

2、修改虚拟机网络配置

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh edit clsn7 </span>
<span style="color: #000000;">修改前：
    </span>&lt;interface type=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">network</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>>
      &lt;mac address=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">52:54:00:42:bf:bc</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
      &lt;source network=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">default</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
      &lt;model type=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">virtio</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
      &lt;address type=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">pci</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> domain=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x0000</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> bus=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x00</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> slot=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x03</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> function=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x0</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
    &lt;/interface><span style="color: #000000;">
修改后：
    </span>&lt;interface type=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">bridge</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>>
      &lt;mac address=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">52:54:00:42:bf:bc</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
      &lt;source bridge=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">br0</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
      &lt;model type=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">virtio</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
      &lt;address type=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">pci</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> domain=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x0000</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> bus=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x00</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> slot=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x03</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span> function=<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">0x0</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>/>
    &lt;/interface></pre>
  </div>
</div>

&nbsp;&nbsp; 查看宿主机网桥

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> brctl show </span>
<span style="color: #000000;">bridge name    bridge id        STP enabled    interfaces
br0        </span>8000<span style="color: #000000;">.000c294d551b    yes        eth0
virbr0     </span>8000.5254006aaa40    yes        virbr0-<span style="color: #000000;">nic
                                vnet0
                                vnet1</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

<p class="ac">
  &nbsp;&nbsp; 查看防火墙规则：
</p>

<div class="cnblogs_code">
  <pre>    [root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> iptables -t nat  -nvL</span>
    Chain PREROUTING (policy ACCEPT 195 packets, 24665<span style="color: #000000;"> bytes)
     pkts bytes target     prot opt </span><span style="color: #0000ff;">in</span><span style="color: #000000;">     out     source               destination         

    Chain INPUT (policy ACCEPT </span>131 packets, 16209<span style="color: #000000;"> bytes)
     pkts bytes target     prot opt </span><span style="color: #0000ff;">in</span><span style="color: #000000;">     out     source               destination         

    Chain OUTPUT (policy ACCEPT </span>272 packets, 24045<span style="color: #000000;"> bytes)
     pkts bytes target     prot opt </span><span style="color: #0000ff;">in</span><span style="color: #000000;">     out     source               destination         

    Chain POSTROUTING (policy ACCEPT </span>272 packets, 24045<span style="color: #000000;"> bytes)
     pkts bytes target     prot opt </span><span style="color: #0000ff;">in</span><span style="color: #000000;">     out     source               destination         
        0     0 RETURN     all  </span>--  *      *       192.168.122.0/24     224.0.0.0/24        
        1   328 RETURN     all  --  *      *       192.168.122.0/24     255.255.255.255     
       29  1740 MASQUERADE  tcp  --  *      *       192.168.122.0/24    !192.168.122.0/24     masq ports: 1024-65535<span style="color: #000000;">
        0     0 MASQUERADE  udp  </span>--  *      *       192.168.122.0/24    !192.168.122.0/24     masq ports: 1024-65535
        3   252 MASQUERADE  all  --  *      *       192.168.122.0/24    !192.168.122.0/24 </pre>
</div>

3、修改kvm虚拟机网卡配置文件

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@clsn7 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> cat /etc/sysconfig/network-scripts/ifcfg-eth0 </span>
TYPE=<span style="color: #000000;">Ethernet
BOOTPROTO</span>=<span style="color: #000000;">static
NAME</span>=<span style="color: #000000;">eth0
DEVICE</span>=<span style="color: #000000;">eth0
ONBOOT</span>=<span style="color: #000000;">yes
IPADDR</span>=10.0.0.110<span style="color: #000000;">
NETMASK</span>=255.255.255.0<span style="color: #000000;">
GATEWAY</span>=10.0.0.254<span style="color: #000000;">
DNS1</span>=223.5.5.5</pre>
  </div>
</div>

测试网络连通性

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@clsn7 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> ping 223.5.5.5 -c1 </span>
PING 223.5.5.5 (223.5.5.5) 56(84<span style="color: #000000;">) bytes of data.
</span>64 bytes <span style="color: #0000ff;">from</span> 223.5.5.5: icmp_seq=1 ttl=128 time=94.4 ms</pre>
  </div>
</div>

## <span id="16_KVM">1.6 KVM虚拟机冷/热迁移</span>

　　在进行迁移之前需要准备一台与KVM配置相同的机器（KVM02）,部署好kvm环境。

### <span id="161">1.6.1 虚拟机冷迁移</span>

　　在kvm02中安装kvm组件

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm02 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> yum install libvirt* virt-* qemu-kvm* -y</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

　　配置桥接网络

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm02 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh iface-bridge eth0 br0</span>
[root@kvm02 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> mkdir -p /data</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

　　将虚拟机关机，导出配置文件

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh dumpxml clsn7 >clsn7.xml</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

　　将虚拟机文件传输到kvm02上

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm data]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> scp -rp  clsn7.xml clsn.qcow2  10.0.0.201:/data</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

　　导入配置文件

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm02 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh define clsn7.xml</span></pre>
  </div>
  
  <p>
    　　启动虚拟机
  </p>
</div>

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm02 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh start clsn7</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

　　查看虚拟机状态

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm02 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virsh list --all </span>
<span style="color: #000000;"> Id    名称                         状态
</span>----------------------------------------------------
 5     clsn7                          running</pre>
  </div>
</div>

&nbsp;　<span style="background-color: #ffff00;">&nbsp; 至此，一次KVM冷迁移就完成了</span>

### <span id="162_virt-managerkvm">1.6.2 virt-manager和kvm虚拟机热迁移（准备）</span>

　　实现kvm虚拟机热迁移核心：共享存储。在这里使用的时NFS共享存储，关于nfs的详情参考：[http://www.cnblogs.com/clsn/p/7694456.html][4]

1、安装virt-manager所需桌面及vnc-server

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> yum groupinstall "GNOME Desktop" -y</span><span style="color: #008000;">
#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> vnc-server端</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> yum install tigervnc-server -y</span><span style="color: #008000;">
#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> virt-manager需要软件</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> yum install openssh-askpass -y</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

2、配置vnc服务

复制vnc配置文件

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> vi /usr/lib/systemd/system/vncserver@.services</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> \cp /usr/lib/systemd/system/vncserver@.service  /usr/lib/systemd/system/vncserver@\:1.service</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

修改配置文件，主要修改<USER>参数。

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> egrep -v "^#|^$" /usr/lib/systemd/system/vncserver@\:1.service</span>
<span style="color: #000000;">[Unit]
Description</span>=<span style="color: #000000;">Remote desktop service (VNC)
After</span>=<span style="color: #000000;">syslog.target network.target
[Service]
Type</span>=<span style="color: #000000;">forking
User</span>=<span style="color: #000000;">root
ExecStartPre</span>=-/usr/bin/vncserver -kill %<span style="color: #000000;">i
ExecStart</span>=/usr/bin/vncserver %<span style="color: #000000;">i
PIDFile</span>=/root/.vnc/%H%<span style="color: #000000;">i.pid
ExecStop</span>=-/usr/bin/vncserver -kill %<span style="color: #000000;">i
[Install]
WantedBy</span>=multi-<span style="color: #000000;">user.target
</span><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 用户为root，家目录为root</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

官方提供修改方法

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> Quick HowTo:</span><span style="color: #008000;">
#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 1. Copy this file to /etc/systemd/system/vncserver@.service</span><span style="color: #008000;">
#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 2. Replace &lt;USER> with the actual user name and edit vncserver</span><span style="color: #008000;">
#</span><span style="color: #008000;">    parameters appropriately</span><span style="color: #008000;">
#</span><span style="color: #008000;">   ("User=&lt;USER>" and "/home/&lt;USER>/.vnc/%H%i.pid")</span><span style="color: #008000;">
#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 3. Run `systemctl daemon-reload`</span><span style="color: #008000;">
#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 4. Run `systemctl enable vncserver@:&lt;display>.service`</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

设置vnc连接时的密码，

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> vncpasswd </span>
<span style="color: #000000;">Password:
Verify:
Would you like to enter a view</span>-only password (y/<span style="color: #000000;">n)? n  
</span><span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> y为创建只读用户，n为非只读用户。</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

启动vnc服务，设置开机自启动

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> systemctl start vncserver@\:1.services</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> systemctl enable vncserver@\:1.services</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

查看密码文件及其他配置文件位置

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> ll ~/.vnc/</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

3、配置NFS存储

安装软件

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> yum install nfs-utils rpcbind -y</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

修改配置文件

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> cat /etc/exports</span>
/data   172.16.1.0/24(rw,sync,all_squash,anonuid=0,anongid=0)</pre>
  </div>
</div>

启动nfs程序

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> systemctl restart rpcbind </span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> systemctl restart nfs</span><span style="color: #008000;">
#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 设置开机自启动</span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> systemctl enable rpcbind </span>
[root@kvm ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> systemctl enable nfs</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

在kvm02上安装nfs

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm02 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;">  yum install nfs-utils rpcbind -y</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

&nbsp;&nbsp; 查看共享信息

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm02 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> showmount -e 172.16.1.240</span>
Export list <span style="color: #0000ff;">for</span> 172.16.1.240<span style="color: #000000;">:
</span>/data 172.16.1.0/24</pre>
  </div>
</div>

&nbsp;&nbsp; 挂载目录

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[root@kvm02 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> mount.nfs 172.16.1.240:/data /data</span><span style="color: #008000;">
#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> 加入开机自启动</span>
[root@kvm02 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> echo  'mount.nfs 172.16.1.240:/data /data' >>/etc/rc.local</span>
[root@kvm02 ~]<span style="color: #008000;">#</span><span style="color: #008000;"> chmod +x /etc/rc.d/rc.local</span></pre>
  </div>
</div>

说明：在热迁移的过程中可能会参数丢包的情况，一般不会超过1个包。

<div>
  <div class="cnblogs_code">
    <pre>[C:\~]$ ping 10.0.0.110 -<span style="color: #000000;">t
来自 </span>10.0.0.110 的回复: 字节=32 时间=1ms TTL=64<span style="color: #000000;">
来自 </span>10.0.0.110 的回复: 字节=32 时间=13ms TTL=64<span style="color: #000000;">
来自 </span>10.0.0.110 的回复: 字节=32 时间=11ms TTL=64<span style="color: #000000;">
请求超时。
来自 </span>10.0.0.110 的回复: 字节=32 时间=4ms TTL=64<span style="color: #000000;">
来自 </span>10.0.0.110 的回复: 字节=32 时间&lt;1ms TTL=64<span style="color: #000000;">
来自 </span>10.0.0.110 的回复: 字节=32 时间&lt;1ms TTL=64</pre>
  </div>
</div>

　　至此，一次热迁移就完成了

## <span id="17_KVM">1.7 KVM链接克隆</span>

链接克隆脚本

<div class="cnblogs_code">
  <pre>#!/bin/<span style="color: #000000;">bash
# kvm link clone scripts  
# user clsn 
# blog: https:</span><span style="color: #008000;">//</span><span style="color: #008000;">www.nmtui.com</span>
# <span style="color: #800080;">2018</span>-<span style="color: #800080;">02</span>-<span style="color: #800080;">06</span><span style="color: #000000;">
###

# init
</span><span style="color: #0000ff;">if</span> [ $# -ne <span style="color: #800080;">2</span><span style="color: #000000;"> ]
  </span><span style="color: #0000ff;">then</span> 
    <span style="color: #0000ff;">echo</span> <span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">Usage: $0 OLD_VMNAME NEW_VMNAME</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
    exit </span><span style="color: #800080;">2</span>
<span style="color: #0000ff;">fi</span><span style="color: #000000;">
LOG</span>=/var/log/<span style="color: #000000;">messages
old_vm</span>=$<span style="color: #800080;">1</span><span style="color: #000000;">
new_vm</span>=$<span style="color: #800080;">2</span><span style="color: #000000;">
new_xml</span>=<span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">/tmp/${new_vm}.xml</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;">
. </span>/etc/init.d/<span style="color: #000000;">functions

# dump old xmlfile 
virsh dumpxml $old_vm </span>><span style="color: #000000;">$new_xml
old_disk</span>=`<span style="color: #0000ff;">awk</span> -F <span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span> <span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">/source file/{print $2}</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #000000;">  $new_xml`
tmp_dir</span>=`<span style="color: #0000ff;">dirname</span><span style="color: #000000;"> $old_disk`
new_disk</span>=${tmp_dir}/<span style="color: #000000;">${new_vm}.qcow2

# </span><span style="color: #0000ff;">make</span><span style="color: #000000;"> link disk 
qemu</span>-img create -f qcow2 -b $old_disk $new_disk &>><span style="color: #000000;"> $LOG

# </span><span style="color: #0000ff;">make</span> over xml <span style="color: #0000ff;">info</span> 
<span style="color: #0000ff;">sed</span> -i <span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">/uuid/d</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #000000;"> $new_xml
</span><span style="color: #0000ff;">sed</span> -i <span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">/mac address/d</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #000000;"> $new_xml
</span><span style="color: #0000ff;">sed</span> -i <span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">2s#</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>$old_vm<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">#</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span>$new_vm<span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">#</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #000000;"> $new_xml
</span><span style="color: #0000ff;">sed</span> -i <span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">s#$old_disk#$new_disk#g</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #000000;"> $new_xml
</span><span style="color: #0000ff;">sed</span> -i <span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #800000;">/source mode/d</span><span style="color: #800000;">'</span><span style="color: #000000;"> $new_xml

# import new xml </span><span style="color: #0000ff;">file</span><span style="color: #000000;">
virsh define $new_xml </span>&>><span style="color: #000000;"> $LOG

# start new vm 
virsh start $new_vm </span>&>><span style="color: #000000;"> $LOG
</span><span style="color: #0000ff;">if</span> [ $? -eq <span style="color: #800080;"></span><span style="color: #000000;"> ]
  </span><span style="color: #0000ff;">then</span><span style="color: #000000;"> 
   action </span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">vmhost $new_vm start</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span>  /bin/<span style="color: #0000ff;">true</span> 
<span style="color: #0000ff;">else</span><span style="color: #000000;"> 
   action </span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">vmhost $new_vm start</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span>  /bin/<span style="color: #0000ff;">false</span>
   <span style="color: #0000ff;">echo</span> <span style="color: #800000;">"</span><span style="color: #800000;">log info : $LOG</span><span style="color: #800000;">"</span>
<span style="color: #0000ff;">fi</span><span style="color: #000000;">

# END
\</span><span style="color: #0000ff;">rm</span> $new_xml</pre>
</div>

说明:

### <span id="171">1.7.1 手动克隆</span>

第一步：复制虚拟磁盘文件  
第二步：修改xml配置文件  
　　1）name  
　　2）uuid  
　　3）虚拟磁盘存储路径  
　　4）mac地址

### <span id="172">1.7.2脚本实现思路</span>

<div class="cnblogs_code">
  <pre><span style="color: #800080;">1</span><span style="color: #000000;">) 备份old_vm的配置文件，并重定向生成一个新的虚拟机配置文件
</span><span style="color: #800080;">2</span><span style="color: #000000;">）取出old_vm的磁盘路径
</span><span style="color: #800080;">3</span><span style="color: #000000;">）创建新的链接磁盘文件
</span><span style="color: #800080;">4</span><span style="color: #000000;">) 修改xml配置文件
</span><span style="color: #800080;">5</span><span style="color: #000000;">) 导入新虚拟机
</span><span style="color: #800080;">6</span>）启动测试</pre>
</div>
